 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Drives Record Fourth Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; July</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;19, 2018 &#151;
</B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, as compared to the corresponding period of last fiscal year: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $30.1&nbsp;billion and increased 17% </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $10.4&nbsp;billion and increased 35% </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $8.9&nbsp;billion GAAP and $8.8&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share was $1.14 GAAP and $1.13 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;We had an incredible year, surpassing $100&nbsp;billion in revenue as a result of our teams&#146; relentless focus on customer success and
the trust customers are placing in Microsoft,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer of Microsoft. &#147;Our early investments in the intelligent cloud and intelligent edge are paying off, and we will continue to expand our reach in large
and growing markets with differentiated innovation.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table reconciles our financial results reported in accordance
with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results. Additional information regarding our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definition is provided below. All
growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:4pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, Carolyn Frantz, deputy general counsel and corporate secretary, and Michael Spencer,
general manager of investor relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The
session may be accessed at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on July&nbsp;19, 2019. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>New Accounting Standards </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We adopted new accounting standards related to revenue recognition and leases effective July&nbsp;1, 2017. The prior periods presented here have
been restated to reflect adoption of these new standards. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Restructuring Expenses.</I> We recorded $306&nbsp;million of restructuring charges primarily related to our sales and marketing
restructuring plan during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>TCJA Impact.</I> We recorded a benefit of $104&nbsp;million during the three months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2018 and a net charge of $13.7&nbsp;billion during the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 related to TCJA. As of June&nbsp;30, 2018, we have not completed our accounting for the tax effects of TCJA. Our net charge is provisional
based on reasonable estimates for those tax effects. Changes to these estimates or new guidance issued by regulators may materially impact our provision for income taxes and effective tax rate in the period in which the adjustments are made. Our
accounting for the tax effects of TCJA will be completed during the measurement period, which should not extend beyond the second fiscal quarter of 2019. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">We have provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures related to restructuring expenses and TCJA to aid investors in better understanding our performance. We believe these <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures aid investors by providing additional insight into our operational performance and help clarify trends affecting our business. For comparability of reporting, management considers <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with GAAP financial results in evaluating business performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be
considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant
Currency </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses
performed excluding the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States
dollars using the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has
provided this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should
not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>FOURTH QUARTER FINANCIAL HIGHLIGHTS </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Please refer to the reconciliation of our GAAP and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results in the table provided above for additional information. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SUMMARY
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $30.1&nbsp;billion and increased 17%, driven by growth across each of our segments. Revenue included a favorable
foreign currency impact of 2%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gross margin was $20.3&nbsp;billion and increased 19%, due to growth across each of our segments. Gross
margin included a favorable foreign currency impact of 3%. Gross margin percentage increased slightly, driven by gross margin percentage improvement in More Personal Computing. Gross margin included a 6 percentage point improvement in commercial
cloud gross margin percentage, primarily from Azure, offset in part by increased Azure sales mix. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was
$10.4&nbsp;billion and increased 35%, driven by growth across each of our segments and a reduction in restructuring expenses. Operating income included a favorable foreign currency impact of 6%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
operating income was $10.4&nbsp;billion and increased 30%, excluding restructuring expenses of $306&nbsp;million in the prior year. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $8.9&nbsp;billion and increased 10%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> net income was $8.8&nbsp;billion and
increased 5%, excluding the net benefit related to TCJA of $104&nbsp;million in the current year and restructuring expenses of $243&nbsp;million in the prior year. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted EPS was $1.14 and increased 11%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> diluted EPS was $1.13 and increased 7%, excluding the
net benefit related to TCJA of $0.01 in the current year and restructuring expenses of $0.03 in the prior year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SEGMENT INFORMATION
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>Productivity and Business Processes </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $1.1&nbsp;billion or 13%, including a favorable foreign currency impact of 3%. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

lower revenue from products licensed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-premises,</FONT> reflecting a continued shift to Office 365 commercial. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gross margin increased $1.3&nbsp;billion or 23%, driven by growth in server products and cloud services revenue and cloud services scale and efficiencies. Gross margin percentage was relatively
unchanged, primarily due to gross margin percentage improvement in Azure, offset in part by an increased mix of cloud offerings. Gross margin included a favorable foreign currency impact of 3%. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating expenses increased $292&nbsp;million or 11%, driven by investments in cloud engineering and commercial sales capacity. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>More Personal Computing </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $1.6&nbsp;billion or 17%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Windows revenue increased $532&nbsp;million or 11%, driven by Windows Commercial and Windows OEM revenue growth. Windows Commercial revenue increased 23%, driven by an increased volume of
multi-year agreements and the mix of products that carry higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-quarter</FONT> revenue recognition. Windows OEM revenue increased 7%. Windows OEM Pro revenue grew 14%, ahead of a strengthening commercial PC
market, driven by a higher mix of premium licenses. Windows OEM <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-Pro</FONT> revenue declined 3%, slightly below the consumer PC market, driven by continued pressure in the entry-level price category.
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gaming revenue increased $643&nbsp;million or 39%, driven by higher revenue from Xbox software and services. Xbox software and services revenue increased 36%, mainly from third-party title
strength. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Surface revenue increased $237&nbsp;million or 25%, driven by strong performance of the latest editions of Surface against a low prior year comparable. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Search advertising revenue increased $183&nbsp;million or 12%. Search advertising revenue, excluding traffic acquisition costs, increased 17%, driven by growth in Bing, primarily due to higher
revenue per search and search volume. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income increased $826&nbsp;million or 38%, including a favorable foreign
currency impact of 6%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

reduction of the U.S. federal statutory tax rate as a result of the TCJA. The prior quarter effective tax rate reflected a $1.8&nbsp;billion benefit related to the utilization of prior years&#146; losses from Microsoft&#146;s phone business that
were not deductible in the years incurred. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate was 18%, excluding the net benefit related to TCJA in the current year. </FONT></P>

income, net, increased $25&nbsp;million, driven by an increase in dividends and interest income and higher net recognized gains on derivatives, offset in part by higher recognized losses from foreign currency remeasurement and lower net recognized
gains from sales of investments. </FONT></P>
